\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/* stb\_image -\/ v2.25 -\/ public domain image loader -\/ http://nothings.org/stb}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{                                  no warranty implied; use at your own risk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{   Do this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{      \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{   before you include this file in *one* C or C++ file to create the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{   // i.e. it should look like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{   \#define STB\_IMAGE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{   \#include "{}stb\_image.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{   You can \#define STBI\_ASSERT(x) before the \#include to avoid using assert.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{   And \#define STBI\_MALLOC, STBI\_REALLOC, and STBI\_FREE to avoid using malloc,realloc,free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{   QUICK NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{      Primarily of interest to game developers and other people who can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{          avoid problematic images and only need the trivial interface}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{      JPEG baseline \& progressive (12 bpc/arithmetic not supported, same as stock IJG lib)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{      PNG 1/2/4/8/16-\/bit-\/per-\/channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{      TGA (not sure what subset, if a subset)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{      BMP non-\/1bpp, non-\/RLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{      PSD (composited view only, no extra channels, 8/16 bit-\/per-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{      GIF (*comp always reports as 4-\/channel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{      HDR (radiance rgbE format)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{      PIC (Softimage PIC)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{      PNM (PPM and PGM binary only)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{      Animated GIF still needs a proper API, but here's one way to do it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{          http://gist.github.com/urraka/685d9a6340b26b830d49}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from memory or through FILE (define STBI\_NO\_STDIO to remove code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ decode from arbitrary I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{comment}{      -\/ SIMD acceleration on x86/x64 (SSE2) and ARM (NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{comment}{   Full documentation under "{}DOCUMENTATION"{} below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{117 \textcolor{comment}{// DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{118 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119 \textcolor{comment}{// Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{120 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 12-\/bit-\/per-\/channel JPEG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no JPEGs with arithmetic coding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ GIF always returns *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{124 \textcolor{comment}{// Basic usage (see HDR discussion below for HDR usage):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{125 \textcolor{comment}{//    int x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{//    unsigned char *data = stbi\_load(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... process data if not NULL ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... x = width, y = height, n = \# 8-\/bit components per pixel ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... replace '0' with '1'..'4' to force that many components per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... but 'n' will always be the number that it would have been if you said 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{//    stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{// Standard parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *x                 -\/-\/ outputs image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *y                 -\/-\/ outputs image height in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *channels\_in\_file  -\/-\/ outputs \# of image components in image file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{//    int desired\_channels   -\/-\/ if non-\/zero, \# of image components requested in result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{// The return value from an image loader is an 'unsigned char *' which points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{// to the pixel data, or NULL on an allocation failure or if the image is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt or invalid. The pixel data consists of *y scanlines of *x pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{// with each pixel consisting of N interleaved 8-\/bit components; the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel pointed to is top-\/left-\/most in the image. There is no padding between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{144 \textcolor{comment}{// image scanlines or between pixels, regardless of format. The number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{// components N is 'desired\_channels' if desired\_channels is non-\/zero, or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file otherwise. If desired\_channels is non-\/zero,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{// *channels\_in\_file has the number of components that \_would\_ have been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{// output otherwise. E.g. if you set desired\_channels to 4, you will always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{// get RGBA output, but you can check *channels\_in\_file to see if it's trivially}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{// opaque because e.g. there were only 3 channels in the source image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{// An output image with N components has the following components interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{// in this order in each pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{//     N=\#comp     components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{//       1           grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{//       2           grey, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{comment}{//       3           red, green, blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{comment}{//       4           red, green, blue, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161 \textcolor{comment}{// If image loading fails for any reason, the return value will be NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{comment}{// and *x, *y, *channels\_in\_file will be unchanged. The function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_failure\_reason() can be queried for an extremely brief, end-\/user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164 \textcolor{comment}{// unfriendly explanation of why the load failed. Define STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165 \textcolor{comment}{// to avoid compiling these strings at all, and STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG to get slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166 \textcolor{comment}{// more user-\/friendly ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{167 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168 \textcolor{comment}{// Paletted PNG, BMP, GIF, and PIC images are automatically depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 \textcolor{comment}{// UNICODE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174 \textcolor{comment}{//   If compiling for Windows and you wish to use Unicode filenames, compile}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175 \textcolor{comment}{//   with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{176 \textcolor{comment}{//       \#define STBI\_WINDOWS\_UTF8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{comment}{//   and pass utf8-\/encoded filenames. Call stbi\_convert\_wchar\_to\_utf8 to convert}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178 \textcolor{comment}{//   Windows wchar\_t filenames to utf8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{comment}{// Philosophy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{184 \textcolor{comment}{// stb libraries are designed with the following priorities:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{185 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186 \textcolor{comment}{//    1. easy to use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187 \textcolor{comment}{//    2. easy to maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{comment}{//    3. good performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{comment}{// Sometimes I let "{}good performance"{} creep up in priority over "{}easy to maintain"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{comment}{// and for best performance I may provide less-\/easy-\/to-\/use APIs that give higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{comment}{// performance, in addition to the easy-\/to-\/use ones. Nevertheless, it's important}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{comment}{// to keep in mind that from the standpoint of you, a client of this library,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{comment}{// all you care about is \#1 and \#3, and stb libraries DO NOT emphasize \#3 above all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{195 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{196 \textcolor{comment}{// Some secondary priorities arise directly from the first two, some of which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{197 \textcolor{comment}{// provide more explicit reasons why performance can't be emphasized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{198 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Portable ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Small source code footprint ("{}easy to maintain"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ No dependencies ("{}ease of use"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{comment}{// I/O callbacks allow you to read from arbitrary sources, like packaged}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{comment}{// files or some other source. Data read from callbacks are processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{// through a small internal buffer (currently 128 bytes) to try to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{// overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{comment}{// The three functions you must define are "{}read"{} (reads some bytes of data),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}skip"{} (skips some bytes of data), "{}eof"{} (reports if the stream is at the end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{comment}{// SIMD support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{comment}{// The JPEG decoder will try to automatically use SIMD kernels on x86 when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{comment}{// supported by the compiler. For ARM Neon support, you must explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{comment}{// request it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 \textcolor{comment}{// (The old do-\/it-\/yourself SIMD API is no longer supported in the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{comment}{// code.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{comment}{// On x86, SSE2 will automatically be used when available based on a run-\/time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227 \textcolor{comment}{// test; if not, the generic C versions are used as a fall-\/back. On ARM targets,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{// the typical path is to have separate builds for NEON and non-\/NEON devices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{// (at least this is true for iOS and Android). Therefore, the NEON support is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{comment}{// toggled by a build flag: define STBI\_NEON to get NEON loops.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{comment}{// If for some reason you do not want to use any of SIMD code, or if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{comment}{// you have issues compiling it, you can disable it entirely by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{// defining STBI\_NO\_SIMD.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{comment}{// HDR image support   (disable by defining STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image supports loading HDR images in general, and currently the Radiance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{comment}{// .HDR file format specifically. You can still load any file through the existing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{comment}{// interface; if you attempt to load an HDR file, it will be automatically remapped}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{// to LDR, assuming gamma 2.2 and an arbitrary scale factor defaulting to 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{// both of these constants can be reconfigured through this interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{comment}{// (note, do not use \_inverse\_ constants; stbi\_image will invert them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, there is a new, parallel interface for loading files as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{comment}{// (linear) floats to preserve the full dynamic range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{255 \textcolor{comment}{//    float *data = stbi\_loadf(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{257 \textcolor{comment}{// If you load LDR images through this interface, those images will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{258 \textcolor{comment}{// be promoted to floating point values, run through the inverse of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{259 \textcolor{comment}{// constants corresponding to the above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{261 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{263 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{264 \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, given a filename (or an open file or memory block-\/-\/see header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{265 \textcolor{comment}{// file for details) containing image data, you can query for the "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{266 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriate"{} interface to use (that is, whether the image is HDR or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{267 \textcolor{comment}{// not), using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{268 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{269 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_is\_hdr(char *filename);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{270 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{271 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{272 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{273 \textcolor{comment}{// iPhone PNG support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{// By default we convert iphone-\/formatted PNGs back to RGB, even though}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{// they are internally encoded differently. You can disable this conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{// by calling stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(0), in which case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{// you will always just get the native iphone "{}format"{} through (which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{// is BGR stored in RGB).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{// Call stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1) as well to force a divide per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{282 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel to remove any premultiplied alpha *only* if the image file explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{283 \textcolor{comment}{// says there's premultiplied data (currently only happens in iPhone images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{284 \textcolor{comment}{// and only if iPhone convert-\/to-\/rgb processing is on).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{643 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(\_\_SSE2\_\_) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{644 \textcolor{comment}{// gcc doesn't support sse2 intrinsics unless you compile with -\/msse2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{645 \textcolor{comment}{// which in turn means it gets to use SSE2 everywhere. This is unfortunate,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{646 \textcolor{comment}{// but previous attempts to provide the SSE2 functions with runtime}}
\DoxyCodeLine{647 \textcolor{comment}{// detection caused numerous issues. The way architecture extensions are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{648 \textcolor{comment}{// exposed in GCC/Clang is, sadly, not really suited for one-\/file libs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{649 \textcolor{comment}{// New behavior: if compiled with -\/msse2, we use SSE2 without any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{650 \textcolor{comment}{// detection; if not, we don't use it at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{651 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{652 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{653 }
\DoxyCodeLine{654 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_MINGW32\_\_) \&\& defined(STBI\_\_X86\_TARGET) \&\& !defined(STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2) \&\& !defined(STBI\_NO\_SIMD)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{655 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that \_\_MINGW32\_\_ doesn't actually mean 32-\/bit, so we have to avoid STBI\_\_X64\_TARGET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{656 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{657 \textcolor{comment}{// 32-\/bit MinGW wants ESP to be 16-\/byte aligned, but this is not in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{658 \textcolor{comment}{// Windows ABI and VC++ as well as Windows DLLs don't maintain that invariant.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{659 \textcolor{comment}{// As a result, enabling SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW is dangerous when not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{660 \textcolor{comment}{// simultaneously enabling "{}-\/mstackrealign"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{661 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{662 \textcolor{comment}{// See https://github.com/nothings/stb/issues/81 for more information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{663 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{664 \textcolor{comment}{// So default to no SSE2 on 32-\/bit MinGW. If you've read this far and added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{665 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/mstackrealign to your build settings, feel free to \#define STBI\_MINGW\_ENABLE\_SSE2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{666 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{667 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{668 }

\DoxyCodeLine{914 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_malloc(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} size)}
\DoxyCodeLine{915 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{916     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_MALLOC(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{917 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{918 }
\DoxyCodeLine{919 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image uses ints pervasively, including for offset calculations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{920 \textcolor{comment}{// therefore the largest decoded image size we can support with the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{921 \textcolor{comment}{// current code, even on 64-\/bit targets, is INT\_MAX. this is not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{922 \textcolor{comment}{// significant limitation for the intended use case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{923 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{924 \textcolor{comment}{// we do, however, need to make sure our size calculations don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{925 \textcolor{comment}{// overflow. hence a few helper functions for size calculations that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{926 \textcolor{comment}{// multiply integers together, making sure that they're non-\/negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{927 \textcolor{comment}{// and no overflow occurs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{928 }
\DoxyCodeLine{929 \textcolor{comment}{// return 1 if the sum is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{930 \textcolor{comment}{// negative terms are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{931 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_addsizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{932 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{933     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{934     \textcolor{comment}{// now 0 <= b <= INT\_MAX, hence also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{935     \textcolor{comment}{// 0 <= INT\_MAX -\/ b <= INTMAX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{936     \textcolor{comment}{// And "{}a + b <= INT\_MAX"{} (which might overflow) is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{937     \textcolor{comment}{// same as a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b (no overflow)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{938     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX -\/ b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{939 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{940 }
\DoxyCodeLine{941 \textcolor{comment}{// returns 1 if the product is valid, 0 on overflow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{942 \textcolor{comment}{// negative factors are considered invalid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{943 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_mul2sizes\_valid(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b)}
\DoxyCodeLine{944 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{945     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a < 0 || b < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{946     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1; \textcolor{comment}{// mul-\/by-\/0 is always safe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{947     \textcolor{comment}{// portable way to check for no overflows in a*b}}
\DoxyCodeLine{948     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} a <= INT\_MAX / b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{949 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{950 }
\DoxyCodeLine{951 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if !defined(STBI\_NO\_JPEG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_PNG) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_TGA) || !defined(STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1128 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_vertical\_flip(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* image, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bytes\_per\_pixel)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1129 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1130     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1131     \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_per\_row = (size\_t)w * bytes\_per\_pixel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1132     stbi\_uc temp[2048];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1133     stbi\_uc* bytes = (stbi\_uc*)image;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1134 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1135     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (row = 0; row < (h >> 1); row++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1136         stbi\_uc* row0 = bytes + row * bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1137         stbi\_uc* row1 = bytes + (h -\/ row -\/ 1) * bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1138         \textcolor{comment}{// swap row0 with row1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1139         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_left = bytes\_per\_row;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1140         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (bytes\_left) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1141             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bytes\_copy = (bytes\_left < \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(temp)) ? bytes\_left : \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1142             memcpy(temp, row0, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1143             memcpy(row0, row1, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1144             memcpy(row1, temp, bytes\_copy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1145             row0 += bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1146             row1 += bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1147             bytes\_left -\/= bytes\_copy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1148         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1149     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1150 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1633 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_NO\_JPEG) \&\& defined(STBI\_NO\_PNG) \&\& defined(STBI\_NO\_BMP) \&\& defined(STBI\_NO\_PSD) \&\& defined(STBI\_NO\_TGA) \&\& defined(STBI\_NO\_GIF) \&\& defined(STBI\_NO\_PIC) \&\& defined(STBI\_NO\_PNM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1634 \textcolor{comment}{// nothing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1635 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1637 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1638 \textcolor{comment}{//  generic converter from built-\/in img\_n to req\_comp}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1639 \textcolor{comment}{//    individual types do this automatically as much as possible (e.g. jpeg}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1640 \textcolor{comment}{//    does all cases internally since it needs to colorspace convert anyway,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1641 \textcolor{comment}{//    and it never has alpha, so very few cases ). png can automatically}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1642 \textcolor{comment}{//    interleave an alpha=255 channel, but falls back to this for other cases}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1643 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1644 \textcolor{comment}{//  assume data buffer is malloced, so malloc a new one and free that one}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1814 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1815 \textcolor{comment}{//  "{}baseline"{} JPEG/JFIF decoder}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1817 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1818 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't support delayed output of y-\/dimension}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1819 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ simple interface (only one output format: 8-\/bit interleaved RGB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1820 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't try to recover corrupt jpegs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1821 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ doesn't allow partial loading, loading multiple at once}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1822 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ still fast on x86 (copying globals into locals doesn't help x86)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1823 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory (full size of all components)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1824 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ non-\/interleaved case requires this anyway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1825 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ allows good upsampling (see next)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1826 \textcolor{comment}{//    high-\/quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1827 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ upsampled channels are bilinearly interpolated, even across blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1828 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ quality integer IDCT derived from IJG's 'slow'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1829 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman; reasonable integer IDCT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1831 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ some SIMD kernels for common paths on targets with SSE2/NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1832 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ uses a lot of intermediate memory, could cache poorly}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1902 \} stbi\_\_jpeg;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1904 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_build\_huffman(stbi\_\_huffman* h, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* count)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1905 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1906     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1907     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1908     \textcolor{comment}{// build size list for each symbol (from JPEG spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1909     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 16; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1910         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < count[i]; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1911             h-\/>size[k++] = (stbi\_uc)(i + 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1912     h-\/>size[k] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1913 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1914     \textcolor{comment}{// compute actual symbols (from jpeg spec)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1915     code = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1916     k = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1917     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 1; j <= 16; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1918         \textcolor{comment}{// compute delta to add to code to compute symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1919         h-\/>delta[j] = k -\/ code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1920         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (h-\/>size[k] == j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1921             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (h-\/>size[k] == j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1922                 h-\/>code[k++] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(code++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1923             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code -\/ 1 >= (1u << j)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad code lengths"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1924         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1925         \textcolor{comment}{// compute largest code + 1 for this size, preshifted as needed later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1926         h-\/>maxcode[j] = code << (16 -\/ j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1927         code <<= 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1928     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1929     h-\/>maxcode[j] = 0xffffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1930 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1931     \textcolor{comment}{// build non-\/spec acceleration table; 255 is flag for not-\/accelerated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1932     memset(h-\/>fast, 255, 1 << FAST\_BITS);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1933     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < k; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1934         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} s = h-\/>size[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1935         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1936             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c = h-\/>code[i] << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1937             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (FAST\_BITS -\/ s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1938             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < m; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1939                 h-\/>fast[c + j] = (stbi\_uc)i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1940             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1941         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1942     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1943     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1944 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1945 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1946 \textcolor{comment}{// build a table that decodes both magnitude and value of small ACs in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1947 \textcolor{comment}{// one go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1948 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_build\_fast\_ac(stbi\_\_int16* fast\_ac, stbi\_\_huffman* h)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1949 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1950     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1951     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < (1 << FAST\_BITS); ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1952         stbi\_uc fast = h-\/>fast[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1953         fast\_ac[i] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1954         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fast < 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1955             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rs = h-\/>values[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1956             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} run = (rs >> 4) \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1957             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} magbits = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1958             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} len = h-\/>size[fast];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1959 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1960             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (magbits \&\& len + magbits <= FAST\_BITS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1961                 \textcolor{comment}{// magnitude code followed by receive\_extend code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1962                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k = ((i << len) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)) >> (FAST\_BITS -\/ magbits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1963                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} m = 1 << (magbits -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1964                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k < m) k += (\string~0U << magbits) + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1965                 \textcolor{comment}{// if the result is small enough, we can fit it in fast\_ac table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1966                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k >= -\/128 \&\& k <= 127)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1967                     fast\_ac[i] = (stbi\_\_int16)((k * 256) + (run * 16) + (len + magbits));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1968             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1969         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1970     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1971 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1973 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}

\DoxyCodeLine{1977         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b == 0xff) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1983                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1987         j-\/>code\_bits += 8;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1994 \textcolor{comment}{// decode a jpeg huffman value from the bitstream}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1999 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2000     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2001 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2002     \textcolor{comment}{// look at the top FAST\_BITS and determine what symbol ID it is,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2003     \textcolor{comment}{// if the code is <= FAST\_BITS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2004     c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS)) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{2013     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2014 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2015     \textcolor{comment}{// naive test is to shift the code\_buffer down so k bits are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2016     \textcolor{comment}{// valid, then test against maxcode. To speed this up, we've}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2017     \textcolor{comment}{// preshifted maxcode left so that it has (16-\/k) 0s at the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2018     \textcolor{comment}{// end; in other words, regardless of the number of bits, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2019     \textcolor{comment}{// wants to be compared against something shifted to have 16;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2020     \textcolor{comment}{// that way we don't need to shift inside the loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2021     temp = j-\/>code\_buffer >> 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2022     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = FAST\_BITS + 1; ; ++k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2023         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp < h-\/>maxcode[k])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2024             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2025     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k == 17) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2026         \textcolor{comment}{// error! code not found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2027         j-\/>code\_bits -\/= 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2028         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2029     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2030 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2031     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (k > j-\/>code\_bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2032         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2033 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2034     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the huffman code to the symbol id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035     c = ((j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ k)) \& stbi\_\_bmask[k]) + h-\/>delta[k];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036     STBI\_ASSERT((((j-\/>code\_buffer) >> (32 -\/ h-\/>size[c])) \& stbi\_\_bmask[h-\/>size[c]]) == h-\/>code[c]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2038     \textcolor{comment}{// convert the id to a symbol}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2039     j-\/>code\_bits -\/= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2040     j-\/>code\_buffer <<= k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2041     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} h-\/>values[c];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2042 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2193 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2194         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>eob\_run) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2195             -\/-\/j-\/>eob\_run;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2196             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2197         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2198 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2199         k = j-\/>spec\_start;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2202             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} c, r, s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2203             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>code\_bits < 16) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(j);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2204             c = (j-\/>code\_buffer >> (32 -\/ FAST\_BITS)) \& ((1 << FAST\_BITS) -\/ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2205             r = fac[c];}

\DoxyCodeLine{2208                 s = r \& 15; \textcolor{comment}{// combined length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2209                 j-\/>code\_buffer <<= s;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2211                 zig = stbi\_\_jpeg\_dezigzag[k++];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2212                 data[zig] = (short)((r >> 8) << shift);}

\DoxyCodeLine{2217                 s = rs \& 15;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2218                 r = rs >> 4;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2221                         j-\/>eob\_run = (1 << r);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2222                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2223                             j-\/>eob\_run += stbi\_\_jpeg\_get\_bits(j, r);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2224                         -\/-\/j-\/>eob\_run;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2225                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2226                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2227                     k += 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2228                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2230                     k += r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2231                     zig = stbi\_\_jpeg\_dezigzag[k++];}

\DoxyCodeLine{2233                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2234             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2235         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (k <= j-\/>spec\_end);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2236     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2238         \textcolor{comment}{// refinement scan for these AC coefficients}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2239 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2240         \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} bit = (short)(1 << j-\/>succ\_low);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2241 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2242         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>eob\_run) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2270                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2271                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2272                         \textcolor{comment}{// r=15 s=0 should write 16 0s, so we just do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2273                         \textcolor{comment}{// a run of 15 0s and then write s (which is 0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2274                         \textcolor{comment}{// so we don't have to do anything special here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2275                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2276                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2282                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2283                         s = -\/bit;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2284                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2285 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2323 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define stbi\_\_f2f(x)  ((int) (((x) * 4096 + 0.5)))}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2326 \textcolor{comment}{// derived from jidctint -\/-\/ DCT\_ISLOW}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2328 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   int t0,t1,t2,t3,p1,p2,p3,p4,p5,x0,x1,x2,x3; \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2330 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   p3 = s6;                                    \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2351 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   t0 = t0*stbi\_\_f2f( 0.298631336f);           \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2364 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_block(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2365 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2366     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, val[64], * v = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2367     stbi\_uc* o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2368     \textcolor{keywordtype}{short}* d = data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2369 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2370     \textcolor{comment}{// columns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2371     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 8; ++i, ++d, ++v) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2372         \textcolor{comment}{// if all zeroes, shortcut -\/-\/ this avoids dequantizing 0s and IDCTing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2373         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (d[8] == 0 \&\& d[16] == 0 \&\& d[24] == 0 \&\& d[32] == 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{2374             \&\& d[40] == 0 \&\& d[48] == 0 \&\& d[56] == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2375             \textcolor{comment}{//    no shortcut                 0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2376             \textcolor{comment}{//    (1|2|3|4|5|6|7)==0          0     seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2377             \textcolor{comment}{//    all separate               -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2378             \textcolor{comment}{//    1 \&\& 2|3 \&\& 4|5 \&\& 6|7:    -\/0.047 seconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2379             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dcterm = d[0] * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2380             v[0] = v[8] = v[16] = v[24] = v[32] = v[40] = v[48] = v[56] = dcterm;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2381         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2382         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2383             STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(d[0], d[8], d[16], d[24], d[32], d[40], d[48], d[56])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2384                 \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12; let's bring them back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2385                 \textcolor{comment}{// down, but keep 2 extra bits of precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2386                 x0 += 512; x1 += 512; x2 += 512; x3 += 512;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2387             v[0] = (x0 + t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2388             v[56] = (x0 -\/ t3) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2389             v[8] = (x1 + t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2390             v[48] = (x1 -\/ t2) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2391             v[16] = (x2 + t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2392             v[40] = (x2 -\/ t1) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2393             v[24] = (x3 + t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2394             v[32] = (x3 -\/ t0) >> 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2395         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2396     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2397 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2398     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0, v = val, o = out; i < 8; ++i, v += 8, o += out\_stride) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2399         \textcolor{comment}{// no fast case since the first 1D IDCT spread components out}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2400         STBI\_\_IDCT\_1D(v[0], v[1], v[2], v[3], v[4], v[5], v[6], v[7])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2401             \textcolor{comment}{// constants scaled things up by 1<<12, plus we had 1<<2 from first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2402             \textcolor{comment}{// loop, plus horizontal and vertical each scale by sqrt(8) so together}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2403             \textcolor{comment}{// we've got an extra 1<<3, so 1<<17 total we need to remove.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2404             \textcolor{comment}{// so we want to round that, which means adding 0.5 * 1<<17,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2405             \textcolor{comment}{// aka 65536. Also, we'll end up with -\/128 to 127 that we want}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2406             \textcolor{comment}{// to encode as 0..255 by adding 128, so we'll add that before the shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2407             x0 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2408         x1 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2409         x2 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2410         x3 += 65536 + (128 << 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2411         \textcolor{comment}{// tried computing the shifts into temps, or'ing the temps to see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2412         \textcolor{comment}{// if any were out of range, but that was slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2413         o[0] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 + t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2414         o[7] = stbi\_\_clamp((x0 -\/ t3) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2415         o[1] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 + t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2416         o[6] = stbi\_\_clamp((x1 -\/ t2) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2417         o[2] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 + t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2418         o[5] = stbi\_\_clamp((x2 -\/ t1) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2419         o[3] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 + t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2420         o[4] = stbi\_\_clamp((x3 -\/ t0) >> 17);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2421     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2422 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2423 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2424 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2425 \textcolor{comment}{// sse2 integer IDCT. not the fastest possible implementation but it}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2428 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_idct\_simd(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_stride, \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} data[64])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2429 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2430     \textcolor{comment}{// This is constructed to match our regular (generic) integer IDCT exactly.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2434     \textcolor{comment}{// dot product constant: even elems=x, odd elems=y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2435 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_const(x,y)  \_mm\_setr\_epi16((x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y),(x),(y))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2437 \textcolor{comment}{// out(0) = c0[even]*x + c0[odd]*y   (c0, x, y 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438 \textcolor{comment}{// out(1) = c1[even]*x + c1[odd]*y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2439 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_rot(out0,out1, x,y,c0,c1) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#lo = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2441 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i c0\#\#hi = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16((x),(y)); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out0\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c0); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2444 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_l = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#lo, c1); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2445 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out1\#\#\_h = \_mm\_madd\_epi16(c0\#\#hi, c1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2446 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2447    \textcolor{comment}{// out = in << 12  (in 16-\/bit, out 32-\/bit)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2448 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_widen(out, in) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2449 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_l = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4); \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2450 \textcolor{preprocessor}{      \_\_m128i out\#\#\_h = \_mm\_srai\_epi32(\_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), (in)), 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2451 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2452    \textcolor{comment}{// wide add}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2453 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define dct\_wadd(out, a, b) \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2457    \textcolor{comment}{// wide sub}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2813 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_MARKER\_none  0xff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2814 \textcolor{comment}{// if there's a pending marker from the entropy stream, return that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2815 \textcolor{comment}{// otherwise, fetch from the stream and get a marker. if there's no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2816 \textcolor{comment}{// marker, return 0xff, which is never a valid marker value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2817 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc stbi\_\_get\_marker(stbi\_\_jpeg* j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2818 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2819     stbi\_uc x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2820     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j-\/>marker != STBI\_\_MARKER\_none) \{ x = j-\/>marker; j-\/>marker = STBI\_\_MARKER\_none; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2821     x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2822     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x != 0xff) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} STBI\_\_MARKER\_none;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2823     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (x == 0xff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2824         x = stbi\_\_get8(j-\/>s); \textcolor{comment}{// consume repeated 0xff fill bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2825     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2826 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2827 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2828 \textcolor{comment}{// in each scan, we'll have scan\_n components, and the order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2829 \textcolor{comment}{// of the components is specified by order[]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2830 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_RESTART(x)     ((x) >= 0xd0 \&\& (x) <= 0xd7)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2831 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2832 \textcolor{comment}{// after a restart interval, stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset the entropy decoder and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2833 \textcolor{comment}{// the dc prediction}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2836     j-\/>code\_bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2837     j-\/>code\_buffer = 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2841     j-\/>todo = j-\/>restart\_interval ? j-\/>restart\_interval : 0x7fffffff;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2842     j-\/>eob\_run = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2843     \textcolor{comment}{// no more than 1<<31 MCUs if no restart\_interal? that's plenty safe,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2844     \textcolor{comment}{// since we don't even allow 1<<30 pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2845 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2846 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2847 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_parse\_entropy\_coded\_data(stbi\_\_jpeg* z)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2848 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2849     stbi\_\_jpeg\_reset(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2850     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!z-\/>progressive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2851         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>scan\_n == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2852             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2853             STBI\_SIMD\_ALIGN(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}, data[64]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2854             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = z-\/>order[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2855             \textcolor{comment}{// non-\/interleaved data, we just need to process one block at a time,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2856             \textcolor{comment}{// in trivial scanline order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2857             \textcolor{comment}{// number of blocks to do just depends on how many actual "{}pixels"{} this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2858             \textcolor{comment}{// component has, independent of interleaved MCU blocking and such}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2859             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].x + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2860             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h = (z-\/>img\_comp[n].y + 7) >> 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2861             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < h; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2862                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2863                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} ha = z-\/>img\_comp[n].ha;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2864                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_jpeg\_decode\_block(z, data, z-\/>huff\_dc + z-\/>img\_comp[n].hd, z-\/>huff\_ac + ha, z-\/>fast\_ac[ha], n, z-\/>dequant[z-\/>img\_comp[n].tq])) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2865                     z-\/>idct\_block\_kernel(z-\/>img\_comp[n].data + z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2 * j * 8 + i * 8, z-\/>img\_comp[n].w2, data);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2866                     \textcolor{comment}{// every data block is an MCU, so countdown the restart interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2867                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (-\/-\/z-\/>todo <= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2868                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>code\_bits < 24) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(z);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2869                         \textcolor{comment}{// if it's NOT a restart, then just bail, so we get corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2870                         \textcolor{comment}{// rather than no data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2871                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!STBI\_\_RESTART(z-\/>marker)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2873                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2874                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2875             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2876             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2877         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2878         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{ \textcolor{comment}{// interleaved}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2880             STBI\_SIMD\_ALIGN(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}, data[64]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2881             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < z-\/>img\_mcu\_y; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < z-\/>img\_mcu\_x; ++i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2895                             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2896                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897                     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2916             \textcolor{comment}{// number of blocks to do just depends on how many actual "{}pixels"{} this}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2931                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2932                     \textcolor{comment}{// every data block is an MCU, so countdown the restart interval}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2933                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (-\/-\/z-\/>todo <= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2934                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>code\_bits < 24) stbi\_\_grow\_buffer\_unsafe(z);}

\DoxyCodeLine{2937                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2938                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2942         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{ \textcolor{comment}{// interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2943             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, k, x, y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2944             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < z-\/>img\_mcu\_y; ++j) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3194         z-\/>img\_comp[i].v = q \& 15;    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!z-\/>img\_comp[i].v || z-\/>img\_comp[i].v > 4) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad V"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt JPEG"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{3196     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3197 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3198     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (scan != STBI\_\_SCAN\_load) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3199 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3200     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(s-\/>img\_x, s-\/>img\_y, s-\/>img\_n, 0)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Image too large to decode"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3201 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3202     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < s-\/>img\_n; ++i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3205     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3206 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3207     \textcolor{comment}{// compute interleaved mcu info}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3208     z-\/>img\_h\_max = h\_max;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3209     z-\/>img\_v\_max = v\_max;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3210     z-\/>img\_mcu\_w = h\_max * 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3211     z-\/>img\_mcu\_h = v\_max * 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3212     \textcolor{comment}{// these sizes can't be more than 17 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3213     z-\/>img\_mcu\_x = (s-\/>img\_x + z-\/>img\_mcu\_w -\/ 1) / z-\/>img\_mcu\_w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214     z-\/>img\_mcu\_y = (s-\/>img\_y + z-\/>img\_mcu\_h -\/ 1) / z-\/>img\_mcu\_h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3215 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3216     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < s-\/>img\_n; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3217         \textcolor{comment}{// number of effective pixels (e.g. for non-\/interleaved MCU)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3218         z-\/>img\_comp[i].x = (s-\/>img\_x * z-\/>img\_comp[i].h + h\_max -\/ 1) / h\_max;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219         z-\/>img\_comp[i].y = (s-\/>img\_y * z-\/>img\_comp[i].v + v\_max -\/ 1) / v\_max;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3220         \textcolor{comment}{// to simplify generation, we'll allocate enough memory to decode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221         \textcolor{comment}{// the bogus oversized data from using interleaved MCUs and their}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222         \textcolor{comment}{// big blocks (e.g. a 16x16 iMCU on an image of width 33); we won't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3223         \textcolor{comment}{// discard the extra data until colorspace conversion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3224         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3225         \textcolor{comment}{// img\_mcu\_x, img\_mcu\_y: <=17 bits; comp[i].h and .v are <=4 (checked earlier)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3226         \textcolor{comment}{// so these muls can't overflow with 32-\/bit ints (which we require)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3227         z-\/>img\_comp[i].w2 = z-\/>img\_mcu\_x * z-\/>img\_comp[i].h * 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228         z-\/>img\_comp[i].h2 = z-\/>img\_mcu\_y * z-\/>img\_comp[i].v * 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3229         z-\/>img\_comp[i].coeff = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230         z-\/>img\_comp[i].raw\_coeff = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3231         z-\/>img\_comp[i].linebuf = NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232         z-\/>img\_comp[i].raw\_data = stbi\_\_malloc\_mad2(z-\/>img\_comp[i].w2, z-\/>img\_comp[i].h2, 15);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3233         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>img\_comp[i].raw\_data == NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3234             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_free\_jpeg\_components(z, i + 1, stbi\_\_err(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3235         \textcolor{comment}{// align blocks for idct using mmx/sse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236         z-\/>img\_comp[i].data = (stbi\_uc*)(((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})z-\/>img\_comp[i].raw\_data + 15) \& \string~15);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (z-\/>progressive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238             \textcolor{comment}{// w2, h2 are multiples of 8 (see above)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3239             z-\/>img\_comp[i].coeff\_w = z-\/>img\_comp[i].w2 / 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3240             z-\/>img\_comp[i].coeff\_h = z-\/>img\_comp[i].h2 / 8;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3246     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3408 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_resample\_row\_hv\_2\_simd(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc* in\_near, stbi\_uc* in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3409 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3410     \textcolor{comment}{// need to generate 2x2 samples for every one in input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3411     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0, t0, t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3412 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3413     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3414         out[0] = out[1] = stbi\_\_div4(3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0] + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3415         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3416     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3417 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3418     t1 = 3 * in\_near[0] + in\_far[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3419     \textcolor{comment}{// process groups of 8 pixels for as long as we can.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3420     \textcolor{comment}{// note we can't handle the last pixel in a row in this loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3421     \textcolor{comment}{// because we need to handle the filter boundary conditions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3422     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < ((w -\/ 1) \& \string~7); i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3424         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426         \_\_m128i zero = \_mm\_setzero\_si128();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3427         \_\_m128i farb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (in\_far + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3428         \_\_m128i nearb = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (in\_near + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429         \_\_m128i farw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(farb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3430         \_\_m128i nearw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(nearb, zero);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431         \_\_m128i diff = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(farw, nearw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3432         \_\_m128i nears = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(nearw, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433         \_\_m128i curr = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3435         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436         \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437         \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439         \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440         \_\_m128i prv0 = \_mm\_slli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441         \_\_m128i nxt0 = \_mm\_srli\_si128(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442         \_\_m128i prev = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(prv0, t1, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443         \_\_m128i next = \_mm\_insert\_epi16(nxt0, 3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3445         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449         \_\_m128i bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450         \_\_m128i curs = \_mm\_slli\_epi16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451         \_\_m128i prvd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3452         \_\_m128i nxtd = \_mm\_sub\_epi16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3453         \_\_m128i curb = \_mm\_add\_epi16(curs, bias);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3454         \_\_m128i even = \_mm\_add\_epi16(prvd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3455         \_\_m128i odd = \_mm\_add\_epi16(nxtd, curb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3456 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3457         \textcolor{comment}{// interleave even and odd pixels, then undo scaling.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3458         \_\_m128i int0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3459         \_\_m128i int1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(even, odd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3460         \_\_m128i de0 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int0, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3461         \_\_m128i de1 = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(int1, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3462 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3463         \textcolor{comment}{// pack and write output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3464         \_\_m128i outv = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(de0, de1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3465         \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + i * 2), outv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3466 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3467         \textcolor{comment}{// load and perform the vertical filtering pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3468         \textcolor{comment}{// this uses 3*x + y = 4*x + (y -\/ x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3469         uint8x8\_t farb = vld1\_u8(in\_far + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3470         uint8x8\_t nearb = vld1\_u8(in\_near + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3471         int16x8\_t diff = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vsubl\_u8(farb, nearb));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3472         int16x8\_t nears = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(nearb, 2));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3473         int16x8\_t curr = vaddq\_s16(nears, diff); \textcolor{comment}{// current row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3474 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3475         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter works the same based on shifted vers of current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476         \textcolor{comment}{// row. "{}prev"{} is current row shifted right by 1 pixel; we need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477         \textcolor{comment}{// insert the previous pixel value (from t1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}next"{} is current row shifted left by 1 pixel, with first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479         \textcolor{comment}{// of next block of 8 pixels added in.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480         int16x8\_t prv0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481         int16x8\_t nxt0 = vextq\_s16(curr, curr, 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482         int16x8\_t prev = vsetq\_lane\_s16(t1, prv0, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483         int16x8\_t next = vsetq\_lane\_s16(3 * in\_near[i + 8] + in\_far[i + 8], nxt0, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3485         \textcolor{comment}{// horizontal filter, polyphase implementation since it's convenient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486         \textcolor{comment}{// even pixels = 3*cur + prev = cur*4 + (prev -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487         \textcolor{comment}{// odd  pixels = 3*cur + next = cur*4 + (next -\/ cur)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488         \textcolor{comment}{// note the shared term.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489         int16x8\_t curs = vshlq\_n\_s16(curr, 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490         int16x8\_t prvd = vsubq\_s16(prev, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491         int16x8\_t nxtd = vsubq\_s16(next, curr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492         int16x8\_t even = vaddq\_s16(curs, prvd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493         int16x8\_t odd = vaddq\_s16(curs, nxtd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3495         \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling and round, then store with even/odd phases interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496         uint8x8x2\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497         o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(even, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498         o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(odd, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499         vst2\_u8(out + i * 2, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3502         \textcolor{comment}{// "{}previous"{} value for next iter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i + 7] + in\_far[i + 7];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3506     t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507     t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508     out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3510     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (++i; i < w; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511         t0 = t1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512         t1 = 3 * in\_near[i] + in\_far[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513         out[i * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t0 + t1 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514         out[i * 2] = stbi\_\_div16(3 * t1 + t0 + 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3516     out[w * 2 -\/ 1] = stbi\_\_div4(t1 + 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3517 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3518     STBI\_NOTUSED(hs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3519 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3520     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3522 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3524 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_resample\_row\_generic(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc* in\_near, stbi\_uc* in\_far, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} hs)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3525 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3526     \textcolor{comment}{// resample with nearest-\/neighbor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3527     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3528     STBI\_NOTUSED(in\_far);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3530         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < hs; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3531             out[i * hs + j] = in\_near[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3532     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3533 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3534 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3535 \textcolor{comment}{// this is a reduced-\/precision calculation of YCbCr-\/to-\/RGB introduced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3536 \textcolor{comment}{// to make sure the code produces the same results in both SIMD and scalar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3537 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define stbi\_\_float2fixed(x)  (((int) ((x) * 4096.0f + 0.5f)) << 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3538 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_row(stbi\_uc* out, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* y, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* pcb, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3539 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3540     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3541     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3542         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3543         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3545         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3546         r = y\_fixed + cr * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547         g = y\_fixed + (cr * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.71414f)) + ((cb * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3548         b = y\_fixed + cb * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3549         r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3550         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3551         b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3552         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3553         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3554         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3555         out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3556         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3557         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3558         out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3559         out += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3560     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3561 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3562 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3563 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(STBI\_SSE2) || defined(STBI\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3564 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_YCbCr\_to\_RGB\_simd(stbi\_uc* out, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* y, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* pcb, stbi\_uc \textcolor{keyword}{const}* pcr, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} step)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3565 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3566     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3567 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3568 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_SSE2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3569     \textcolor{comment}{// step == 3 is pretty ugly on the final interleave, and i'm not convinced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3570     \textcolor{comment}{// it's useful in practice (you wouldn't use it for textures, for example).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3571     \textcolor{comment}{// so just accelerate step == 4 case.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3572     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3573         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3574         \_\_m128i signflip = \_mm\_set1\_epi8(-\/0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3575         \_\_m128i cr\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3576         \_\_m128i cr\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3577         \_\_m128i cb\_const0 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3578         \_\_m128i cb\_const1 = \_mm\_set1\_epi16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3579         \_\_m128i y\_bias = \_mm\_set1\_epi8((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char})(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char})128);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3580         \_\_m128i xw = \_mm\_set1\_epi16(255); \textcolor{comment}{// alpha channel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3581 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3582         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3583             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3584             \_\_m128i y\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (y + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3585             \_\_m128i cr\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (pcr + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3586             \_\_m128i cb\_bytes = \_mm\_loadl\_epi64((\_\_m128i*) (pcb + i));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3587             \_\_m128i cr\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cr\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3588             \_\_m128i cb\_biased = \_mm\_xor\_si128(cb\_bytes, signflip); \textcolor{comment}{// -\/128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3589 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3590             \textcolor{comment}{// unpack to short (and left-\/shift cr, cb by 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3591             \_\_m128i yw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(y\_bias, y\_bytes);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3592             \_\_m128i crw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cr\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3593             \_\_m128i cbw = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(\_mm\_setzero\_si128(), cb\_biased);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3594 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3595             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3596             \_\_m128i yws = \_mm\_srli\_epi16(yw, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3597             \_\_m128i cr0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cr\_const0, crw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3598             \_\_m128i cb0 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cb\_const0, cbw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3599             \_\_m128i cb1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3600             \_\_m128i cr1 = \_mm\_mulhi\_epi16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3601             \_\_m128i rws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cr0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3602             \_\_m128i gwt = \_mm\_add\_epi16(cb0, yws);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3603             \_\_m128i bws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3604             \_\_m128i gws = \_mm\_add\_epi16(gwt, cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3605 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3606             \textcolor{comment}{// descale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3607             \_\_m128i rw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3608             \_\_m128i bw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3609             \_\_m128i gw = \_mm\_srai\_epi16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3610 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3611             \textcolor{comment}{// back to byte, set up for transpose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3612             \_\_m128i brb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(rw, bw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613             \_\_m128i gxb = \_mm\_packus\_epi16(gw, xw);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3614 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3615             \textcolor{comment}{// transpose to interleave channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616             \_\_m128i t0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617             \_\_m128i t1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi8(brb, gxb);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618             \_\_m128i o0 = \_mm\_unpacklo\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619             \_\_m128i o1 = \_mm\_unpackhi\_epi16(t0, t1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3621             \textcolor{comment}{// store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3622             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + 0), o0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623             \_mm\_storeu\_si128((\_\_m128i*) (out + 16), o1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624             out += 32;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3625         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3628 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3629 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef STBI\_NEON}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3630     \textcolor{comment}{// in this version, step=3 support would be easy to add. but is there demand?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3631     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (step == 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632         \textcolor{comment}{// this is a fairly straightforward implementation and not super-\/optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3633         uint8x8\_t signflip = vdup\_n\_u8(0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634         int16x8\_t cr\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.40200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3635         int16x8\_t cr\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.71414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3636         int16x8\_t cb\_const0 = vdupq\_n\_s16(-\/(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(0.34414f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3637         int16x8\_t cb\_const1 = vdupq\_n\_s16((\textcolor{keywordtype}{short})(1.77200f * 4096.0f + 0.5f));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3638 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3639         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i + 7 < count; i += 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3640             \textcolor{comment}{// load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3641             uint8x8\_t y\_bytes = vld1\_u8(y + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3642             uint8x8\_t cr\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcr + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3643             uint8x8\_t cb\_bytes = vld1\_u8(pcb + i);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3644             int8x8\_t cr\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cr\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3645             int8x8\_t cb\_biased = vreinterpret\_s8\_u8(vsub\_u8(cb\_bytes, signflip));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3646 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3647             \textcolor{comment}{// expand to s16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3648             int16x8\_t yws = vreinterpretq\_s16\_u16(vshll\_n\_u8(y\_bytes, 4));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3649             int16x8\_t crw = vshll\_n\_s8(cr\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3650             int16x8\_t cbw = vshll\_n\_s8(cb\_biased, 7);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3651 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3652             \textcolor{comment}{// color transform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3653             int16x8\_t cr0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3654             int16x8\_t cb0 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3655             int16x8\_t cr1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(crw, cr\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3656             int16x8\_t cb1 = vqdmulhq\_s16(cbw, cb\_const1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3657             int16x8\_t rws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cr0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3658             int16x8\_t gws = vaddq\_s16(vaddq\_s16(yws, cb0), cr1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3659             int16x8\_t bws = vaddq\_s16(yws, cb1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3661             \textcolor{comment}{// undo scaling, round, convert to byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3662             uint8x8x4\_t o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663             o.val[0] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(rws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3664             o.val[1] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(gws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665             o.val[2] = vqrshrun\_n\_s16(bws, 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666             o.val[3] = vdup\_n\_u8(255);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3668             \textcolor{comment}{// store, interleaving r/g/b/a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3669             vst4\_u8(out, o);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3670             out += 8 * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3672     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3673 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3674 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3675     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i < count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3676         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_fixed = (y[i] << 20) + (1 << 19); \textcolor{comment}{// rounding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3677         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3678         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cr = pcr[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3679         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cb = pcb[i] -\/ 128;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3680         r = y\_fixed + cr * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.40200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3681         g = y\_fixed + cr * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.71414f) + ((cb * -\/stbi\_\_float2fixed(0.34414f)) \& 0xffff0000);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3682         b = y\_fixed + cb * stbi\_\_float2fixed(1.77200f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3683         r >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3684         g >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3685         b >>= 20;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3686         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})r > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) r = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} r = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3687         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})g > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g < 0) g = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} g = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3688         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned})b > 255) \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (b < 0) b = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} b = 255; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3689         out[0] = (stbi\_uc)r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3690         out[1] = (stbi\_uc)g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3691         out[2] = (stbi\_uc)b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3692         out[3] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3693         out += step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3694     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3695 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3696 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3698 \textcolor{comment}{// set up the kernels}}
