\DoxyCodeLine{3958 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain zlib decode    v0.2  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3959 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3960 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all input must be provided in an upfront buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3961 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all output is written to a single output buffer (can malloc/realloc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3962 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3963 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3964 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3965 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_ZLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3966 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3967 \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/way is faster to check than jpeg huffman, but slow way is slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3968 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS  9 }\textcolor{comment}{// accelerate all cases in default tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3969 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define STBI\_\_ZFAST\_MASK  ((1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS) -\/ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3970 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3971 \textcolor{comment}{// zlib-\/style huffman encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3972 \textcolor{comment}{// (jpegs packs from left, zlib from right, so can't share code)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3973 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3974 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3975     stbi\_\_uint16 fast[1 << STBI\_\_ZFAST\_BITS];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3976     stbi\_\_uint16 firstcode[16];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3977     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} maxcode[17];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3978     stbi\_\_uint16 firstsymbol[16];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3979     stbi\_uc  size[288];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3980     stbi\_\_uint16 value[288];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3981 \} stbi\_\_zhuffman;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3982 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3983 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3984 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3985     n = ((n \& 0xAAAA) >> 1) | ((n \& 0x5555) << 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3986     n = ((n \& 0xCCCC) >> 2) | ((n \& 0x3333) << 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3987     n = ((n \& 0xF0F0) >> 4) | ((n \& 0x0F0F) << 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3988     n = ((n \& 0xFF00) >> 8) | ((n \& 0x00FF) << 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3989     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3990 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3991 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3992 stbi\_inline \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_bit\_reverse(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} v, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bits)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3993 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3994     STBI\_ASSERT(bits <= 16);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3995     \textcolor{comment}{// to bit reverse n bits, reverse 16 and shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3996     \textcolor{comment}{// e.g. 11 bits, bit reverse and shift away 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3997     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_bitreverse16(v) >> (16 -\/ bits);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3998 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4000 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_zbuild\_huffman(stbi\_\_zhuffman* z, \textcolor{keyword}{const} stbi\_uc* sizelist, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4442 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain "{}baseline"{} PNG decoder   v0.10  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4443 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ only 8-\/bit samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ no CRC checking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4446 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ allocates lots of intermediate memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4447 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/ avoids problem of streaming data between subsystems}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4449 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4536     img\_width\_bytes = (((img\_n * x * depth) + 7) >> 3);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4537     img\_len = (img\_width\_bytes + 1) * y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4538 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4539     \textcolor{comment}{// we used to check for exact match between raw\_len and img\_len on non-\/interlaced PNGs,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4540     \textcolor{comment}{// but issue \#276 reported a PNG in the wild that had extra data at the end (all zeros),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4541     \textcolor{comment}{// so just check for raw\_len < img\_len always.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4543 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4544     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < y; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4545         stbi\_uc* cur = a-\/>out + stride * j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4546         stbi\_uc* prior;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4547         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} filter = *raw++;}

\DoxyCodeLine{4549         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (filter > 4)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4555             filter\_bytes = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4556             width = img\_width\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4557         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4560         \textcolor{comment}{// if first row, use special filter that doesn't sample previous row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4561         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j == 0) filter = first\_row\_filter[filter];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4562 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4563         \textcolor{comment}{// handle first byte explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4564         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k = 0; k < filter\_bytes; ++k) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4565             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (filter) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4566             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_none: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4567             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_sub: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4568             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_up: cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + prior[k]); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4569             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBI\_\_F\_avg: cur[k] = STBI\_\_BYTECAST(raw[k] + (prior[k] >> 1)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4573             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4574         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4575 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4578                 cur[img\_n] = 255; \textcolor{comment}{// first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4579             raw += img\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4580             cur += out\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4581             prior += out\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4582         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4586                 cur[filter\_bytes + 1] = 255; \textcolor{comment}{// first pixel bottom byte}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4590             prior += output\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4591         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4645     \textcolor{comment}{// we make a separate pass to expand bits to pixels; for performance,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4646     \textcolor{comment}{// this could run two scanlines behind the above code, so it won't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4647     \textcolor{comment}{// intefere with filtering but will still be in the cache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4648     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth < 8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4649         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < y; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4650             stbi\_uc* cur = a-\/>out + stride * j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4651             stbi\_uc* in = a-\/>out + stride * j + x * out\_n -\/ img\_width\_bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4652             \textcolor{comment}{// unpack 1/2/4-\/bit into a 8-\/bit buffer. allows us to keep the common 8-\/bit path optimal at minimal cost for 1/2/4-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4653             \textcolor{comment}{// png guarante byte alignment, if width is not multiple of 8/4/2 we'll decode dummy trailing data that will be skipped in the later loop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4654             stbi\_uc scale = (color == 0) ? stbi\_\_depth\_scale\_table[depth] : 1; \textcolor{comment}{// scale grayscale values to 0..255 range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4655 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4656             \textcolor{comment}{// note that the final byte might overshoot and write more data than desired.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4657             \textcolor{comment}{// we can allocate enough data that this never writes out of memory, but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4658             \textcolor{comment}{// could also overwrite the next scanline. can it overwrite non-\/empty data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4659             \textcolor{comment}{// on the next scanline? yes, consider 1-\/pixel-\/wide scanlines with 1-\/bit-\/per-\/pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4660             \textcolor{comment}{// so we need to explicitly clamp the final ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4661 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4662             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 4) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4690                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4701                 \textcolor{comment}{// insert alpha = 255}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4702                 cur = a-\/>out + stride * j;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4703                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (img\_n == 1) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4707                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4708                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4719         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4720     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4721     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (depth == 16) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{4737 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_create\_png\_image(stbi\_\_png* a, stbi\_uc* image\_data, stbi\_\_uint32 image\_data\_len, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_n, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} depth, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} color, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} interlaced)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4738 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4739     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bytes = (depth == 16 ? 2 : 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4740     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_bytes = out\_n * bytes;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4741     stbi\_uc* \textcolor{keyword}{final};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4742     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4743     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!interlaced)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4744         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_create\_png\_image\_raw(a, image\_data, image\_data\_len, out\_n, a-\/>s-\/>img\_x, a-\/>s-\/>img\_y, depth, color);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4745 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4746     \textcolor{comment}{// de-\/interlacing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4747     \textcolor{keyword}{final} = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc\_mad3(a-\/>s-\/>img\_x, a-\/>s-\/>img\_y, out\_bytes, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4748     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (p = 0; p < 7; ++p) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4749         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} xorig[] = \{ 0,4,0,2,0,1,0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4750         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} yorig[] = \{ 0,0,4,0,2,0,1 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4751         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} xspc[] = \{ 8,8,4,4,2,2,1 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4752         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} yspc[] = \{ 8,8,8,4,4,2,2 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4753         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i, j, x, y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4754         \textcolor{comment}{// pass1\_x[4] = 0, pass1\_x[5] = 1, pass1\_x[12] = 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4755         x = (a-\/>s-\/>img\_x -\/ xorig[p] + xspc[p] -\/ 1) / xspc[p];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4756         y = (a-\/>s-\/>img\_y -\/ yorig[p] + yspc[p] -\/ 1) / yspc[p];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4757         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x \&\& y) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4758             stbi\_\_uint32 img\_len = ((((a-\/>s-\/>img\_n * x * depth) + 7) >> 3) + 1) * y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4759             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_create\_png\_image\_raw(a, image\_data, image\_data\_len, out\_n, x, y, depth, color)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4760                 STBI\_FREE(\textcolor{keyword}{final});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4761                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4762             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4763             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < y; ++j) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4764                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < x; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4765                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_y = j * yspc[p] + yorig[p];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4766                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_x = i * xspc[p] + xorig[p];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4767                     memcpy(\textcolor{keyword}{final} + out\_y * a-\/>s-\/>img\_x * out\_bytes + out\_x * out\_bytes,}
\DoxyCodeLine{4768                         a-\/>out + (j * x + i) * out\_bytes, out\_bytes);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4769                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4770             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4771             STBI\_FREE(a-\/>out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4772             image\_data += img\_len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4773             image\_data\_len -\/= img\_len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4774         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4775     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4776     a-\/>out = \textcolor{keyword}{final};}

\DoxyCodeLine{4781 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_compute\_transparency(stbi\_\_png* z, stbi\_uc tc[3], \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} out\_n)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4783     stbi\_\_context* s = z-\/>s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4784     stbi\_\_uint32 i, pixel\_count = s-\/>img\_x * s-\/>img\_y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4785     stbi\_uc* p = z-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4786 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4787     \textcolor{comment}{// compute color-\/based transparency, assuming we've}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4788     \textcolor{comment}{// already got 255 as the alpha value in the output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4789     STBI\_ASSERT(out\_n == 2 || out\_n == 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4790 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4791     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (out\_n == 2) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{5667 \textcolor{comment}{// read 16bit value and convert to 24bit RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5668 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_tga\_read\_rgb16(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_uc* out)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5669 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5670     stbi\_\_uint16 px = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5671     stbi\_\_uint16 fiveBitMask = 31;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5672     \textcolor{comment}{// we have 3 channels with 5bits each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5673     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r = (px >> 10) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5674     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} g = (px >> 5) \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5675     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} b = px \& fiveBitMask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5676     \textcolor{comment}{// Note that this saves the data in RGB(A) order, so it doesn't need to be swapped later}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5677     out[0] = (stbi\_uc)((r * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5678     out[1] = (stbi\_uc)((g * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5679     out[2] = (stbi\_uc)((b * 255) / 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5680 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5681     \textcolor{comment}{// some people claim that the most significant bit might be used for alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5682     \textcolor{comment}{// (possibly if an alpha-\/bit is set in the "{}image descriptor byte"{})}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5683     \textcolor{comment}{// but that only made 16bit test images completely translucent..}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5684     \textcolor{comment}{// so let's treat all 15 and 16bit TGAs as RGB with no alpha.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5685 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5686 }

\DoxyCodeLine{5867         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* tga\_pixel = tga\_data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5868         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < tga\_width * tga\_height; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5869         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5870             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp = tga\_pixel[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5871             tga\_pixel[0] = tga\_pixel[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5872             tga\_pixel[2] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5873             tga\_pixel += tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5874         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5875     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5876 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5877     \textcolor{comment}{// convert to target component count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5878     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != tga\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5879         tga\_data = stbi\_\_convert\_format(tga\_data, tga\_comp, req\_comp, tga\_width, tga\_height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5880 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5881     \textcolor{comment}{//   the things I do to get rid of an error message, and yet keep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5882     \textcolor{comment}{//   Microsoft's C compilers happy... [8\string^(}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5883     tga\_palette\_start = tga\_palette\_len = tga\_palette\_bits =}
\DoxyCodeLine{5884         tga\_x\_origin = tga\_y\_origin = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5885     STBI\_NOTUSED(tga\_palette\_start);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5886     \textcolor{comment}{//   OK, done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5887     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} tga\_data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5888 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5889 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5890 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5891 \textcolor{comment}{// *************************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5892 \textcolor{comment}{// Photoshop PSD loader -\/-\/ PD by Thatcher Ulrich, integration by Nicolas Schulz, tweaked by STB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5893 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5894 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef STBI\_NO\_PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5895 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_test(stbi\_\_context* s)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5896 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5897     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r = (stbi\_\_get32be(s) == 0x38425053);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5898     stbi\_\_rewind(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5899     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5900 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5901 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5902 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_uc* p, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5903 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5904     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count, nleft, len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5905 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5906     count = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5907     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((nleft = pixelCount -\/ count) > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5908         len = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5909         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5910             \textcolor{comment}{// No-\/op.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5911         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5912         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len < 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5913             \textcolor{comment}{// Copy next len+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5914             len++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5915             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5916             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5917             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5918                 *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5919                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5920                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5921             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5922         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5923         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5924             stbi\_uc   val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5925             \textcolor{comment}{// Next -\/len+1 bytes in the dest are replicated from next source byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5926             \textcolor{comment}{// (Interpret len as a negative 8-\/bit int.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5927             len = 257 -\/ len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5928             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > nleft) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// corrupt data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5929             val = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5930             count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5931             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5932                 *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5933                 p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5934                 len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5935             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5936         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5937     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5938 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5939     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5940 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5941 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5942 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_psd\_load(stbi\_\_context* s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_\_result\_info* ri, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bpc)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5943 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5944     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelCount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5945     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channelCount, compression;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5946     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} channel, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5947     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} bitdepth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5948     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} w, h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5949     stbi\_uc* out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5950     STBI\_NOTUSED(ri);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5951 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5952     \textcolor{comment}{// Check identifier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5953     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get32be(s) != 0x38425053)   \textcolor{comment}{// "{}8BPS"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5954         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}not PSD"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5956     \textcolor{comment}{// Check file type version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5957     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5958         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong version"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported version of PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5959 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5960     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip 6 reserved bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5961     stbi\_\_skip(s, 6);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5962 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5963     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the number of channels (R, G, B, A, etc).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5964     channelCount = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5965     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount < 0 || channelCount > 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5966         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong channel count"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Unsupported number of channels in PSD image"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5967 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5968     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the rows and columns of the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5969     h = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5970     w = stbi\_\_get32be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5971 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5972     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the depth is 8 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5973     bitdepth = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5974     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth != 8 \&\& bitdepth != 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5975         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}unsupported bit depth"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD bit depth is not 8 or 16 bit"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5977     \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the color mode is RGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5978     \textcolor{comment}{// Valid options are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5979     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: Bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5980     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: Grayscale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5981     \textcolor{comment}{//   2: Indexed color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5982     \textcolor{comment}{//   3: RGB color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5983     \textcolor{comment}{//   4: CMYK color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5984     \textcolor{comment}{//   7: Multichannel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5985     \textcolor{comment}{//   8: Duotone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5986     \textcolor{comment}{//   9: Lab color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5987     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_get16be(s) != 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5988         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong color format"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD is not in RGB color format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{5989 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5990     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the Mode Data.  (It's the palette for indexed color; other info for other modes.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5991     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5992 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5993     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the image resources.  (resolution, pen tool paths, etc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5994     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5995 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5996     \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the reserved data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5997     stbi\_\_skip(s, stbi\_\_get32be(s));}
\DoxyCodeLine{5998 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5999     \textcolor{comment}{// Find out if the data is compressed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6000     \textcolor{comment}{// Known values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6001     \textcolor{comment}{//   0: no compression}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6002     \textcolor{comment}{//   1: RLE compressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6003     compression = stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6004     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression > 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6005         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad compression"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD has an unknown compression format"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6006 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6007     \textcolor{comment}{// Check size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6008     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, w, h, 0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{6009         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt PSD"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6010 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6011     \textcolor{comment}{// Create the destination image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6012 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6013     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!compression \&\& bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6014         out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc\_mad3(8, w, h, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6015         ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel = 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6016     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6017     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6018         out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * w * h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6019 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6020     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!out) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6021     pixelCount = w * h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6022 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6023     \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the data to zero.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6024     \textcolor{comment}{//memset( out, 0, pixelCount * 4 );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6025 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6026     \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, the image data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6027     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6028         \textcolor{comment}{// RLE as used by .PSD and .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6029         \textcolor{comment}{// Loop until you get the number of unpacked bytes you are expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6030         \textcolor{comment}{//     Read the next source byte into n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6031         \textcolor{comment}{//     If n is between 0 and 127 inclusive, copy the next n+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6032         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is between -\/127 and -\/1 inclusive, copy the next byte -\/n+1 times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6033         \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is 128, noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6034         \textcolor{comment}{// Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6035 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6036         \textcolor{comment}{// The RLE-\/compressed data is preceded by a 2-\/byte data count for each row in the data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6037         \textcolor{comment}{// which we're going to just skip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6038         stbi\_\_skip(s, h * channelCount * 2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6039 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6040         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6041         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6042             stbi\_uc* p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6043 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6044             p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6045             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6046                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6047                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6048                     *p = (channel == 3 ? 255 : 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6049             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6050             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6051                 \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6052                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_psd\_decode\_rle(s, p, pixelCount)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6053                     STBI\_FREE(out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6054                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}corrupt"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}bad RLE data"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6055                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6056             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6057         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6058 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6059     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6060     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6061         \textcolor{comment}{// We're at the raw image data.  It's each channel in order (Red, Green, Blue, Alpha, ...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6062         \textcolor{comment}{// where each channel consists of an 8-\/bit (or 16-\/bit) value for each pixel in the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6063 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6064         \textcolor{comment}{// Read the data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6065         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6066             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6067                 \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6068                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16 \&\& bpc == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6069                     stbi\_\_uint16* q = ((stbi\_\_uint16*)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6070                     stbi\_\_uint16 val = channel == 3 ? 65535 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6071                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6072                         *q = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6073                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6074                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6075                     stbi\_uc* p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6076                     stbi\_uc val = channel == 3 ? 255 : 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6077                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6078                         *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6079                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6080             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6081             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6082                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{    \textcolor{comment}{// output bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6083                     stbi\_\_uint16* q = ((stbi\_\_uint16*)out) + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6084                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, q += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6085                         *q = (stbi\_\_uint16)stbi\_\_get16be(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6086                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6087                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6088                     stbi\_uc* p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6089                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bitdepth == 16) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// input bpc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6090                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6091                             *p = (stbi\_uc)(stbi\_\_get16be(s) >> 8);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6092                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6093                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6094                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++, p += 4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6095                             *p = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6096                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6097                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6098             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6099         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6100     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6102     \textcolor{comment}{// remove weird white matte from PSD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6103     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channelCount >= 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6104         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6105             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w * h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6106                 stbi\_\_uint16* pixel = (stbi\_\_uint16*)out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6107                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 65535) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6108                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 65535.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6109                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6110                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 65535.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6111                     pixel[0] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6112                     pixel[1] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6113                     pixel[2] = (stbi\_\_uint16)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6114                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6115             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6116         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6117         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6118             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < w * h; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6119                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* pixel = out + 4 * i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6120                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pixel[3] != 0 \&\& pixel[3] != 255) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6121                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = pixel[3] / 255.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6122                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ra = 1.0f / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6123                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inv\_a = 255.0f * (1 -\/ ra);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6124                     pixel[0] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[0] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6125                     pixel[1] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[1] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6126                     pixel[2] = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(pixel[2] * ra + inv\_a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6127                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6128             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6129         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6130     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6131 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6132     \textcolor{comment}{// convert to desired output format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6133     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp \&\& req\_comp != 4) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6134         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ri-\/>bits\_per\_channel == 16)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6135             out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_convert\_format16((stbi\_\_uint16*)out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6136         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6137             out = stbi\_\_convert\_format(out, 4, req\_comp, w, h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6138         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (out == NULL) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out; \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_\_convert\_format frees input on failure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6139     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6140 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6141     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (comp) *comp = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6142     *y = h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6143     *x = w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6144 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6145     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6146 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6147 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6486         p[1] = c[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6487         p[2] = c[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6488         p[3] = c[3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6489     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6490     g-\/>cur\_x += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6491 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6492     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>cur\_x >= g-\/>max\_x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6493         g-\/>cur\_x = g-\/>start\_x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6494         g-\/>cur\_y += g-\/>step;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6495 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6496         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (g-\/>cur\_y >= g-\/>max\_y \&\& g-\/>parse > 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6497             g-\/>step = (1 << g-\/>parse) * g-\/>line\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6498             g-\/>cur\_y = g-\/>start\_y + (g-\/>step >> 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6499             -\/-\/g-\/>parse;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6500         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6501     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6502 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6503 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6504 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_process\_gif\_raster(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_\_gif* g)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6505 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6506     stbi\_uc lzw\_cs;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6507     stbi\_\_int32 len, init\_code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6508     stbi\_\_uint32 first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6509     stbi\_\_int32 codesize, codemask, avail, oldcode, bits, valid\_bits, clear;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6510     stbi\_\_gif\_lzw* p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6511 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6512     lzw\_cs = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6513     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (lzw\_cs > 12) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6514     clear = 1 << lzw\_cs;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6515     first = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6516     codesize = lzw\_cs + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6517     codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6518     bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6519     valid\_bits = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6520     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (init\_code = 0; init\_code < clear; init\_code++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6521         g-\/>codes[init\_code].prefix = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6522         g-\/>codes[init\_code].first = (stbi\_uc)init\_code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6523         g-\/>codes[init\_code].suffix = (stbi\_uc)init\_code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6524     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6525 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6526     \textcolor{comment}{// support no starting clear code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6527     avail = clear + 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6528     oldcode = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6529 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6530     len = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6531     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (;;) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6532         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (valid\_bits < codesize) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6533             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6534                 len = stbi\_\_get8(s); \textcolor{comment}{// start new block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6535                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6536                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} g-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6537             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6538             -\/-\/len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6539             bits |= (stbi\_\_int32)stbi\_\_get8(s) << valid\_bits;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6540             valid\_bits += 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6541         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6542         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6543             stbi\_\_int32 code = bits \& codemask;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6544             bits >>= codesize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6545             valid\_bits -\/= codesize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6546             \textcolor{comment}{// @OPTIMIZE: is there some way we can accelerate the non-\/clear path?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6547             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == clear) \{  \textcolor{comment}{// clear code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6548                 codesize = lzw\_cs + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6549                 codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6550                 avail = clear + 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6551                 oldcode = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6552                 first = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6553             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6554             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == clear + 1) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// end of stream code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6555                 stbi\_\_skip(s, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6556                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((len = stbi\_\_get8(s)) > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6557                     stbi\_\_skip(s, len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6558                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} g-\/>out;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6559             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6560             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code <= avail) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6561                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (first) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6562                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}no clear code"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6563                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6564 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6565                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (oldcode >= 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6566                     p = \&g-\/>codes[avail++];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6567                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (avail > 8192) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6568                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too many codes"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6569                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6570 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6571                     p-\/>prefix = (stbi\_\_int16)oldcode;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6572                     p-\/>first = g-\/>codes[oldcode].first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6573                     p-\/>suffix = (code == avail) ? p-\/>first : g-\/>codes[code].first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6574                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6575                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code == avail)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6576                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}illegal code in raster"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6577 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6578                 stbi\_\_out\_gif\_code(g, (stbi\_\_uint16)code);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6579 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6580                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((avail \& codemask) == 0 \&\& avail <= 0x0FFF) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6581                     codesize++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6582                     codemask = (1 << codesize) -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6583                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6584 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6585                 oldcode = code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6586             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6587             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6588                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}illegal code in raster"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corrupt GIF"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6589             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6590         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6591     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6592 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6594 \textcolor{comment}{// this function is designed to support animated gifs, although stb\_image doesn't support it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6595 \textcolor{comment}{// two back is the image from two frames ago, used for a very specific disposal format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6596 \textcolor{keyword}{static} stbi\_uc* stbi\_\_gif\_load\_next(stbi\_\_context* s, stbi\_\_gif* g, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp, stbi\_uc* two\_back)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6597 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6598     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dispose;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6599     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} first\_frame;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6600     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pi;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6601     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pcount;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6602     STBI\_NOTUSED(req\_comp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6603 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6604     \textcolor{comment}{// on first frame, any non-\/written pixels get the background colour (non-\/transparent)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6605     first\_frame = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6606     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>out == 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6607         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_gif\_header(s, g, comp, 0)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0; \textcolor{comment}{// stbi\_\_g\_failure\_reason set by stbi\_\_gif\_header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6608         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!stbi\_\_mad3sizes\_valid(4, g-\/>w, g-\/>h, 0))}
\DoxyCodeLine{6609             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}too large"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}GIF image is too large"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6610         pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6611         g-\/>out = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6612         g-\/>background = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6613         g-\/>history = (stbi\_uc*)stbi\_\_malloc(pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6614         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!g-\/>out || !g-\/>background || !g-\/>history)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6615             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} stbi\_\_errpuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}outofmem"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Out of memory"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{6616 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6617         \textcolor{comment}{// image is treated as "{}transparent"{} at the start -\/ ie, nothing overwrites the current background;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6618         \textcolor{comment}{// background colour is only used for pixels that are not rendered first frame, after that "{}background"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6619         \textcolor{comment}{// color refers to the color that was there the previous frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6620         memset(g-\/>out, 0x00, 4 * pcount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6621         memset(g-\/>background, 0x00, 4 * pcount); \textcolor{comment}{// state of the background (starts transparent)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6622         memset(g-\/>history, 0x00, pcount);        \textcolor{comment}{// pixels that were affected previous frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6623         first\_frame = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6624     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6625     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6626         \textcolor{comment}{// second frame -\/ how do we dispoase of the previous one?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6627         dispose = (g-\/>eflags \& 0x1C) >> 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6628         pcount = g-\/>w * g-\/>h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6629 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6630         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((dispose == 3) \&\& (two\_back == 0)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6631             dispose = 2; \textcolor{comment}{// if I don't have an image to revert back to, default to the old background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6632         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6633 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6634         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dispose == 3) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// use previous graphic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6635             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (pi = 0; pi < pcount; ++pi) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6636                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>history[pi]) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6637                     memcpy(\&g-\/>out[pi * 4], \&two\_back[pi * 4], 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6638                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6639             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6640         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6641         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dispose == 2) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6642             \textcolor{comment}{// restore what was changed last frame to background before that frame;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6643             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (pi = 0; pi < pcount; ++pi) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6644                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>history[pi]) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6645                     memcpy(\&g-\/>out[pi * 4], \&g-\/>background[pi * 4], 4);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6646                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6647             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6648         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6649         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6650             \textcolor{comment}{// This is a non-\/disposal case eithe way, so just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6651             \textcolor{comment}{// leave the pixels as is, and they will become the new background}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6652             \textcolor{comment}{// 1: do not dispose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6653             \textcolor{comment}{// 0:  not specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6654         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6655 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6656         \textcolor{comment}{// background is what out is after the undoing of the previou frame;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6657         memcpy(g-\/>background, g-\/>out, 4 * g-\/>w * g-\/>h);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6658     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6659 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6660     \textcolor{comment}{// clear my history;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6661     memset(g-\/>history, 0x00, g-\/>w * g-\/>h);        \textcolor{comment}{// pixels that were affected previous frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6662 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6663     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (;;) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6664         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} tag = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6665         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (tag) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6666         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0x2C: \textcolor{comment}{/* Image Descriptor */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6667         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6668             stbi\_\_int32 x, y, w, h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6669             stbi\_uc* o;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6670 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6671             x = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6672             y = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6673             w = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6674             h = stbi\_\_get16le(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6675             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((x + w) > (g-\/>w)) || ((y + h) > (g-\/>h)))}

\DoxyCodeLine{6677 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6678             g-\/>line\_size = g-\/>w * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6679             g-\/>start\_x = x * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6680             g-\/>start\_y = y * g-\/>line\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6681             g-\/>max\_x = g-\/>start\_x + w * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6682             g-\/>max\_y = g-\/>start\_y + h * g-\/>line\_size;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6684             g-\/>cur\_y = g-\/>start\_y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6685 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6686             \textcolor{comment}{// if the width of the specified rectangle is 0, that means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6687             \textcolor{comment}{// we may not see *any* pixels or the image is malformed;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6688             \textcolor{comment}{// to make sure this is caught, move the current y down to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6689             \textcolor{comment}{// max\_y (which is what out\_gif\_code checks).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6690             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (w == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6691                 g-\/>cur\_y = g-\/>max\_y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6692 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6693             g-\/>lflags = stbi\_\_get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6694 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6695             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (g-\/>lflags \& 0x40) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6731 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6732         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0x21: \textcolor{comment}{// Comment Extension.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6736             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (ext == 0xF9) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// Graphic Control Extension.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6756                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6757                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6761                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6767         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6768 }

\DoxyCodeLine{6775     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6778 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* stbi\_\_load\_gif\_main(stbi\_\_context* s, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}** delays, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* y, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* z, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* comp, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6779 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6780     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbi\_\_gif\_test(s)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6781         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} layers = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6782         stbi\_uc* u = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6783         stbi\_uc* out = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6784         stbi\_uc* two\_back = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6785         stbi\_\_gif g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6786         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stride;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6787         memset(\&g, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(g));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6788         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (delays) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6789             *delays = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6790         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6791 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6792         \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6793             u = stbi\_\_gif\_load\_next(s, \&g, comp, req\_comp, two\_back);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6794             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (u == (stbi\_uc*)s) u = 0;  \textcolor{comment}{// end of animated gif marker}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6795 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6796             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (u) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6797                 *x = g.w;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6798                 *y = g.h;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6799                 ++layers;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6800                 stride = g.w * g.h * 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6801 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6802                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (out) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6803                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* tmp = (stbi\_uc*)STBI\_REALLOC(out, layers * stride);}

\DoxyCodeLine{6814                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6815                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6820                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6821                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6825                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6844     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6934 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbi\_\_hdr\_convert(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* output, stbi\_uc* input, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} req\_comp)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6935 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6936     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (input[3] != 0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6937         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6938         \textcolor{comment}{// Exponent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6939         f1 = (float)ldexp(1.0f, input[3] -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(128 + 8));}
\DoxyCodeLine{6940         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp <= 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6941             output[0] = (input[0] + input[1] + input[2]) * f1 / 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6942         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6943             output[0] = input[0] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6944             output[1] = input[1] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6945             output[2] = input[2] * f1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6946         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6947         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 2) output[1] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6948         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_comp == 4) output[3] = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6949     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6950     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6951         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (req\_comp) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6952         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4: output[3] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6953         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 3: output[0] = output[1] = output[2] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6954             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6955         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2: output[1] = 1; \textcolor{comment}{/* fallthrough */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6956         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1: output[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6957             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6958         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6959     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6960 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6961 }
